<!-- JS: Assign form, test proxy, rotate, live polling -->
<script>
  function toggleAssignForm() {
    const wrapper = document.getElementById('assign-form-wrapper');
    const chevron = document.getElementById('assign-chevron');
    wrapper.classList.toggle('hidden');
    chevron.classList.toggle('rotate-180');
  }

  function toggleSelectAll(el) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.account-checkbox').forEach(cb => { cb.checked = el.checked; });
    updateSelectedCount();
  }

  function updateSelectedCount() {
    const checked = document.querySelectorAll('.account-checkbox:checked').length;
    const el = document.getElementById('selected-count');
    el.textContent = checked > 0 ? checked + ' selected' : '';

    // Sync hidden inputs for the assign form
    const container = document.getElementById('selected-accounts-container');
    container.innerHTML = '';
    document.querySelectorAll('.account-checkbox:checked').forEach(cb => {
      const input = document.createElement('input');
      input.type = 'hidden';
      input.name = 'account_ids';
      input.value = cb.value;
      container.appendChild(input);
    });
  }

  async function rotateIp(name) {
    const btn = document.getElementById('rotate-btn-' + name);
    if (!btn) return;
    const original = btn.textContent;
    btn.textContent = 'Rotating...';
    btn.disabled = true;
    btn.classList.add('opacity-50');
    try {
      const resp = await fetch('/proxies/' + name + '/rotate', { method: 'POST' });
      const data = await resp.json();
      if (data.ok) {
        btn.textContent = 'Rotated \u2713';
        btn.classList.remove('opacity-50', 'text-purple-600', 'bg-purple-50');
        btn.classList.add('text-emerald-600', 'bg-emerald-50');
      } else {
        btn.textContent = data.error || 'Failed';
        btn.classList.remove('opacity-50', 'text-purple-600', 'bg-purple-50');
        btn.classList.add('text-red-600', 'bg-red-50');
      }
    } catch (e) {
      btn.textContent = 'Error';
      btn.classList.add('text-red-600');
    }
    setTimeout(() => {
      btn.textContent = original;
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.classList.remove('opacity-50', 'text-emerald-600', 'bg-emerald-50', 'text-red-600', 'bg-red-50');
      btn.classList.add('text-purple-600', 'bg-purple-50');
    }, 3000);
  }

  async function testProxy(name) {
    const btn = document.getElementById('test-btn-' + name);
    if (!btn) return;
    const original = btn.textContent;
    btn.textContent = 'Testing...';
    btn.disabled = true;
    btn.classList.add('opacity-50');
    try {
      const resp = await fetch('/proxies/test/' + name, { method: 'POST' });
      const data = await resp.json();
      const testedEl = document.getElementById('tested-' + name);
      if (data.ok) {
        btn.textContent = 'Pass \u2713';
        btn.classList.remove('opacity-50', 'text-blue-600', 'bg-blue-50');
        btn.classList.add('text-emerald-600', 'bg-emerald-50');
        if (testedEl) testedEl.innerHTML = '<span class="text-emerald-600">Pass</span> <span class="text-gray-400 ml-1">' + data.response_bytes + 'B</span>';
      } else {
        btn.textContent = 'Fail \u2717';
        btn.classList.remove('opacity-50', 'text-blue-600', 'bg-blue-50');
        btn.classList.add('text-red-600', 'bg-red-50');
        if (testedEl) testedEl.innerHTML = '<span class="text-red-600" title="' + (data.error || '') + '">Fail</span>';
      }
    } catch (e) {
      btn.textContent = 'Error';
      btn.classList.add('text-red-600');
    }
    setTimeout(() => {
      btn.textContent = original;
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.classList.remove('opacity-50', 'text-emerald-600', 'bg-emerald-50', 'text-red-600', 'bg-red-50');
      btn.classList.add('text-blue-600', 'bg-blue-50');
    }, 5000);
  }

  // Poll health every 10s
  setInterval(async () => {
    try {
      const resp = await fetch('/api/proxies/health');
      const data = await resp.json();
      document.getElementById('stat-proxied').textContent = data.proxied_count;
      document.getElementById('stat-healthy').textContent = data.healthy_count;
      document.getElementById('stat-failing').textContent = data.failing_count;
    } catch {}
  }, 10000);
</script>
